ECK120012871	1122659	1122674	caaaggataaGCGGAAACGTTTTCCTttgcacgaaa	When the CTP level within the cell is high relative to the level of GTP, the <i>pyrC</i> gene is transcribed from a start site that allows formation of a secondary structure within the 5' end of the mRNA.
